### Write - 2026-04-12 06:14:20 UTC [08:14:20 CEST]

**User Request:** yes

**Tool:** Write
**Input:** ```json
{
  "file_path": "<AWS_SECRET_REDACTED>ckfill-raw-observations.js",
  "content": "#!/usr/bin/env node\n/**\n * Backfill [Raw] observations by re-summarizing them through the LLM CLI proxy.\n * Run from the coding project root: node scripts/backfill-raw-observations.js\n */\nimport Database from 'better-sqlite3';\nimport path from 'path';\nimport { fileURLToPath } from 'url';\n\nconst __dirname = path.dirname(fileURLToPath(import.<COMPANY_NAME_REDACTED>.url));\nconst DB_PATH = path.resolve(__dirname, '../.observations/observations.db');\nconst PROXY_PORT = process.env.LLM_CLI_PROXY_PORT || '12435';\nconst PROXY_URL = `http://localhost:${PROXY_PORT}/api/complete`;\nconst BATCH_DELAY_MS = 2000;\n\nconst db = new Database(DB_PATH);\n\nconst rawObs = db.prepare(`\n  SELECT id, summary, messages, metadata, created_at\n  FROM observations\n  WHERE summary LIKE '[Raw] % messages%'\n  ORDER BY created_at ASC\n`).all();\n\nprocess.stderr.write(`Found ${rawObs.length} [Raw] observations to backfill\\n`);\n\nlet success = 0, failed = 0, skipped = 0;\n\nfor (let i = 0; i < rawObs.length; i++) {\n  const obs = rawObs[i];\n\n  let messages;\n  try { messages = JSON.parse(obs.messages); }\n  catch { skipped++; continue; }\n\n  if (!messages || messages.length < 2) { skipped++; continue; }\n\n  let metadata = {};\n  try { metadata = JSON.parse(obs.metadata || '{}'); } catch { /* ignore */ }\n  const projectName = metadata.project || 'coding';\n\n  const exchangeBlock = messages\n    .map(m => `<${m.role}>\\n${m.content}\\n</${m.role}>`)\n    .join('\\n');\n\n  const modifiedFiles = metadata.modifiedFiles || [];\n  let artifactHint = '';\n  if (modifiedFiles.length > 0) {\n    artifactHint = `\\n\\nGROUND TRUTH — Files modified/created:\\n` +\n      modifiedFiles.map(f => `  - edited ${f}`).join('\\n');\n  }\n\n  const requestBody = {\n    messages: [\n      {\n        role: 'system',\n        content: `You produce structured observation summaries from coding exchanges.\\n` +\n          `The developer is working in the \"${projectName}\" project.\\n\\n` +\n          'Respond using ONLY this template:\\n\\n' +\n          'Intent: [what the developer asked]\\n' +\n          'Approach: [solution strategy — 1-4 sentences]\\n' +\n          'Artifacts: [files modified/created with verb, or \"none\"]\\n' +\n          'Result: [concrete outcome — 1-4 sentences]\\n\\n' +\n          'If no real work, respond: \"No actionable content.\"' +\n          (artifactHint || ''),\n      },\n      {\n        role: 'user',\n        content: `<project>${projectName}</project>\\n<exchange>\\n${exchangeBlock}\\n</exchange>\\n\\nProduce the observation summary.`,\n      },\n    ],\n  };\n\n  try {\n    const response = await fetch(PROXY_URL, {\n      method: 'POST',\n      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },\n      body: JSON.stringify(requestBody),\n      signal: AbortSignal.timeout(45000),\n    });\n\n    if (!response.ok) {\n      const errBody = await response.text();\n      process.stderr.write(`  [${i+1}/${rawObs.length}] ERR ${response.status}: ${errBody.slice(0,60)}\\n`);\n      failed++;\n      continue;\n    }\n\n    const result = await response.json();\n    const summary = result.content;\n\n    if (!summary || summary.length < 10) { skipped++; continue; }\n\n    const <USER_ID_REDACTED> = summary.toLowerCase().includes('no actionable content') ? 'low' : 'normal';\n    const llmMeta = {\n      ...metadata,\n      llmModel: result.model || null,\n      llmProvider: result.provider || null,\n      llmTokens: result.tokens || null,\n      llmLatencyMs: result.latencyMs || null,\n    };\n\n    db.prepare(`UPDATE observations SET summary = ?, metadata = ?, <USER_ID_REDACTED> = ? WHERE id = ?`)\n      .run(summary, JSON.stringify(llmMeta), <USER_ID_REDACTED>, obs.id);\n\n    process.stderr.write(`  [${i+1}/${rawObs.length}] ${<USER_ID_REDACTED> === 'low' ? 'LOW' : 'OK'}: ${obs.created_at.slice(0,19)} — ${summary.slice(0,50)}\\n`);\n    success++;\n  } catch (err) {\n    process.stderr.write(`  [${i+1}/${rawObs.length}] FAIL: ${err.message}\\n`);\n    failed++;\n  }\n\n  if (i < rawObs.length - 1) {\n    await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, BATCH_DELAY_MS));\n  }\n}\n\nprocess.stderr.write(`\\nDone: ${success} updated, ${failed} failed, ${skipped} skipped\\n`);\ndb.close();\n"
}
```

### Write - 2026-04-12 06:14:20 UTC [08:14:20 CEST]

**User Request:** yes

**Tool:** Write
**Input:** ```json
{
  "file_path": "/tmp/backfill-observations.js",
  "content": "/**\n * Backfill [Raw] observations by re-summarizing them through the LLM proxy.\n * Reads the stored messages from the DB, calls the proxy, updates the summary.\n */\nimport Database from 'better-sqlite3';\nimport path from 'path';\n\nconst DB_PATH = path.resolve('/Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/coding/.observations/observations.db');\nconst PROXY_PORT = process.env.LLM_CLI_PROXY_PORT || '12435';\nconst PROXY_URL = `http://localhost:${PROXY_PORT}/api/complete`;\nconst BATCH_DELAY_MS = 2000; // Rate limit between calls\n\nconst db = new Database(DB_PATH);\n\n// Get all [Raw] observations that have stored messages\nconst rawObs = db.prepare(`\n  SELECT id, summary, messages, metadata, created_at\n  FROM observations\n  WHERE summary LIKE '[Raw] % messages%'\n  ORDER BY created_at ASC\n`).all();\n\nprocess.stderr.write(`Found ${rawObs.length} [Raw] observations to backfill\\n`);\n\nlet success = 0;\nlet failed = 0;\nlet skipped = 0;\n\nfor (let i = 0; i < rawObs.length; i++) {\n  const obs = rawObs[i];\n\n  // Parse stored messages\n  let messages;\n  try {\n    messages = JSON.parse(obs.messages);\n  } catch (_e) {\n    process.stderr.write(`  [${i+1}/${rawObs.length}] SKIP: cannot parse messages for ${obs.id}\\n`);\n    skipped++;\n    continue;\n  }\n\n  if (!messages || messages.length < 2) {\n    skipped++;\n    continue;\n  }\n\n  // Parse metadata for project name\n  let metadata = {};\n  try {\n    metadata = JSON.parse(obs.metadata || '{}');\n  } catch (_e) {\n    // ignore\n  }\n  const projectName = metadata.project || 'coding';\n\n  // Build exchange block\n  const exchangeBlock = messages\n    .map(m => `<${m.role}>\\n${m.content}\\n</${m.role}>`)\n    .join('\\n');\n\n  // Build ground-truth file list from metadata\n  const modifiedFiles = metadata.modifiedFiles || [];\n  const readFiles = metadata.readFiles || [];\n  let artifactHint = '';\n  if (modifiedFiles.length > 0) {\n    artifactHint = `\\n\\nGROUND TRUTH — Files modified/created by tool calls (use these for the Artifacts line):\\n` +\n      modifiedFiles.map(f => `  - edited ${f}`).join('\\n');\n  }\n\n  const requestBody = {\n    messages: [\n      {\n        role: 'system',\n        content: `You produce structured observation summaries from coding exchanges.\\n` +\n          `CRITICAL CONTEXT: The developer is working in the \"${projectName}\" project.\\n\\n` +\n          'Respond using ONLY this template — nothing else:\\n\\n' +\n          'Intent: [what the developer actually asked or requested]\\n' +\n          'Approach: [architectural decisions, solution strategy — 1-4 sentences]\\n' +\n          'Artifacts: [list each file modified/created/deleted with verb. Write \"none\" if no files were touched]\\n' +\n          'Result: [the concrete solution or outcome — 1-4 sentences]\\n\\n' +\n          'Constraints:\\n' +\n          '- Your ENTIRE response must be these 4 labeled lines.\\n' +\n          '- Never reproduce code, commands, or file contents.\\n' +\n          '- If the exchange has no real work (greetings, \"yes\", \"proceed\"), respond with only: \"No actionable content.\"' +\n          (artifactHint || ''),\n      },\n      {\n        role: 'user',\n        content: `<project>${projectName}</project>\\n<exchange>\\n${exchangeBlock}\\n</exchange>\\n\\nProduce the observation summary.`,\n      },\n    ],\n  };\n\n  try {\n    const response = await fetch(PROXY_URL, {\n      method: 'POST',\n      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },\n      body: JSON.stringify(requestBody),\n      signal: AbortSignal.timeout(45000),\n    });\n\n    if (!response.ok) {\n      const errBody = await response.text();\n      process.stderr.write(`  [${i+1}/${rawObs.length}] ERROR ${response.status}: ${errBody.slice(0,80)}\\n`);\n      failed++;\n      continue;\n    }\n\n    const result = await response.json();\n    const summary = result.content;\n\n    if (!summary || summary.length < 10) {\n      process.stderr.write(`  [${i+1}/${rawObs.length}] SKIP: empty summary\\n`);\n      skipped++;\n      continue;\n    }\n\n    // Skip \"No actionable content\" — these are low-value\n    if (summary.toLowerCase().includes('no actionable content')) {\n      // Update to mark as processed but low-value\n      db.prepare(`UPDATE observations SET summary = ?, <USER_ID_REDACTED> = 'low' WHERE id = ?`)\n        .run(summary, obs.id);\n      process.stderr.write(`  [${i+1}/${rawObs.length}] LOW: ${obs.created_at.slice(0,19)}\\n`);\n      success++;\n      continue;\n    }\n\n    // Update the observation with the new summary and LLM metadata\n    const llmMeta = {\n      ...metadata,\n      llmModel: result.model || null,\n      llmProvider: result.provider || null,\n      llmTokens: result.tokens || null,\n      llmLatencyMs: result.latencyMs || null,\n    };\n\n    db.prepare(`UPDATE observations SET summary = ?, metadata = ?, <USER_ID_REDACTED> = 'normal' WHERE id = ?`)\n      .run(summary, JSON.stringify(llmMeta), obs.id);\n\n    process.stderr.write(`  [${i+1}/${rawObs.length}] OK: ${obs.created_at.slice(0,19)} — ${summary.slice(0,60)}\\n`);\n    success++;\n\n  } catch (err) {\n    process.stderr.write(`  [${i+1}/${rawObs.length}] FAIL: ${err.message}\\n`);\n    failed++;\n  }\n\n  // Rate limit\n  if (i < rawObs.length - 1) {\n    await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, BATCH_DELAY_MS));\n  }\n}\n\nprocess.stderr.write(`\\nBackfill complete: ${success} updated, ${failed} failed, ${skipped} skipped\\n`);\ndb.close();\n"
}
```

**Result:** ✅ Success
**Output:** ```
File created successfully at: /tmp/backfill-observations.js

'low' : 'normal';\n    const llmMeta = {\n      ...metadata,\n      llmModel: result.model || null,\n      llmProvider: result.provider || null,\n      llmTokens: result.tokens || null,\n      llmLatencyMs: result.latencyMs || null,\n    };\n\n    db.prepare(`UPDATE observations SET summary = ?, metadata = ?, <USER_ID_REDACTED> = ? WHERE id = ?`)\n      .run(summary, JSON.stringify(llmMeta), <USER_ID_REDACTED>, obs.id);\n\n    process.stderr.write(`  [${i+1}/${rawObs.length}] ${<USER_ID_REDACTED> === 'low' ? 'LOW' : 'OK'}: ${obs.created_at.slice(0,19)} — ${summary.slice(0,50)}\\n`);\n    success++;\n  } catch (err) {\n    process.stderr.write(`  [${i+1}/${rawObs.length}] FAIL: ${err.message}\\n`);\n    failed++;\n  }\n\n  if (i < rawObs.length - 1) {\n    await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, BATCH_DELAY_MS));\n  }\n}\n\nprocess.stderr.write(`\\nDone: ${success} updated, ${failed} failed, ${skipped} skipped\\n`);\ndb.close();\n"
}
```

### Write - 2026-04-12 06:14:20 UTC [08:14:20 CEST]

**User Request:** yes

**Tool:** Write
**Input:** ```json
{
  "file_path": "/tmp/backfill-observations.js",
  "content": "/**\n * Backfill [Raw] observations by re-summarizing them through the LLM proxy.\n * Reads the stored messages from the DB, calls the proxy, updates the summary.\n */\nimport Database from 'better-sqlite3';\nimport path from 'path';\n\nconst DB_PATH = path.resolve('/Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/coding/.observations/observations.db');\nconst PROXY_PORT = process.env.LLM_CLI_PROXY_PORT || '12435';\nconst PROXY_URL = `http://localhost:${PROXY_PORT}/api/complete`;\nconst BATCH_DELAY_MS = 2000; // Rate limit between calls\n\nconst db = new Database(DB_PATH);\n\n// Get all [Raw] observations that have stored messages\nconst rawObs = db.prepare(`\n  SELECT id, summary, messages, metadata, created_at\n  FROM observations\n  WHERE summary LIKE '[Raw] % messages%'\n  ORDER BY created_at ASC\n`).all();\n\nprocess.stderr.write(`Found ${rawObs.length} [Raw] observations to backfill\\n`);\n\nlet success = 0;\nlet failed = 0;\nlet skipped = 0;\n\nfor (let i = 0; i < rawObs.length; i++) {\n  const obs = rawObs[i];\n\n  // Parse stored messages\n  let messages;\n  try {\n    messages = JSON.parse(obs.messages);\n  } catch (_e) {\n    process.stderr.write(`  [${i+1}/${rawObs.length}] SKIP: cannot parse messages for ${obs.id}\\n`);\n    skipped++;\n    continue;\n  }\n\n  if (!messages || messages.length < 2) {\n    skipped++;\n    continue;\n  }\n\n  // Parse metadata for project name\n  let metadata = {};\n  try {\n    metadata = JSON.parse(obs.metadata || '{}');\n  } catch (_e) {\n    // ignore\n  }\n  const projectName = metadata.project || 'coding';\n\n  // Build exchange block\n  const exchangeBlock = messages\n    .map(m => `<${m.role}>\\n${m.content}\\n</${m.role}>`)\n    .join('\\n');\n\n  // Build ground-truth file list from metadata\n  const modifiedFiles = metadata.modifiedFiles || [];\n  const readFiles = metadata.readFiles || [];\n  let artifactHint = '';\n  if (modifiedFiles.length > 0) {\n    artifactHint = `\\n\\nGROUND TRUTH — Files modified/created by tool calls (use these for the Artifacts line):\\n` +\n      modifiedFiles.map(f => `  - edited ${f}`).join('\\n');\n  }\n\n  const requestBody = {\n    messages: [\n      {\n        role: 'system',\n        content: `You produce structured observation summaries from coding exchanges.\\n` +\n          `CRITICAL CONTEXT: The developer is working in the \"${projectName}\" project.\\n\\n` +\n          'Respond using ONLY this template — nothing else:\\n\\n' +\n          'Intent: [what the developer actually asked or requested]\\n' +\n          'Approach: [architectural decisions, solution strategy — 1-4 sentences]\\n' +\n          'Artifacts: [list each file modified/created/deleted with verb. Write \"none\" if no files were touched]\\n' +\n          'Result: [the concrete solution or outcome — 1-4 sentences]\\n\\n' +\n          'Constraints:\\n' +\n          '- Your ENTIRE response must be these 4 labeled lines.\\n' +\n          '- Never reproduce code, commands, or file contents.\\n' +\n          '- If the exchange has no real work (greetings, \"yes\", \"proceed\"), respond with only: \"No actionable content.\"' +\n          (artifactHint || ''),\n      },\n      {\n        role: 'user',\n        content: `<project>${projectName}</project>\\n<exchange>\\n${exchangeBlock}\\n</exchange>\\n\\nProduce the observation summary.`,\n      },\n    ],\n  };\n\n  try {\n    const response = await fetch(PROXY_URL, {\n      method: 'POST',\n      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },\n      body: JSON.stringify(requestBody),\n      signal: AbortSignal.timeout(45000),\n    });\n\n    if (!response.ok) {\n      const errBody = await response.text();\n      process.stderr.write(`  [${i+1}/${rawObs.length}] ERROR ${response.status}: ${errBody.slice(0,80)}\\n`);\n      failed++;\n      continue;\n    }\n\n    const result = await response.json();\n    const summary = result.content;\n\n    if (!summary || summary.length < 10) {\n      process.stderr.write(`  [${i+1}/${rawObs.length}] SKIP: empty summary\\n`);\n      skipped++;\n      continue;\n    }\n\n    // Skip \"No actionable content\" — these are low-value\n    if (summary.toLowerCase().includes('no actionable content')) {\n      // Update to mark as processed but low-value\n      db.prepare(`UPDATE observations SET summary = ?, <USER_ID_REDACTED> = 'low' WHERE id = ?`)\n        .run(summary, obs.id);\n      process.stderr.write(`  [${i+1}/${rawObs.length}] LOW: ${obs.created_at.slice(0,19)}\\n`);\n      success++;\n      continue;\n    }\n\n    // Update the observation with the new summary and LLM metadata\n    const llmMeta = {\n      ...metadata,\n      llmModel: result.model || null,\n      llmProvider: result.provider || null,\n      llmTokens: result.tokens || null,\n      llmLatencyMs: result.latencyMs || null,\n    };\n\n    db.prepare(`UPDATE observations SET summary = ?, metadata = ?, <USER_ID_REDACTED> = 'normal' WHERE id = ?`)\n      .run(summary, JSON.stringify(llmMeta), obs.id);\n\n    process.stderr.write(`  [${i+1}/${rawObs.length}] OK: ${obs.created_at.slice(0,19)} — ${summary.slice(0,60)}\\n`);\n    success++;\n\n  } catch (err) {\n    process.stderr.write(`  [${i+1}/${rawObs.length}] FAIL: ${err.message}\\n`);\n    failed++;\n  }\n\n  // Rate limit\n  if (i < rawObs.length - 1) {\n    await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, BATCH_DELAY_MS));\n  }\n}\n\nprocess.stderr.write(`\\nBackfill complete: ${success} updated, ${failed} failed, ${skipped} skipped\\n`);\ndb.close();\n"
}
```

**Result:** ✅ Success
**Output:** ```
File created successfully at: /tmp/backfill-observations.js
```

  "file_path": "<AWS_SECRET_REDACTED>ckfill-raw-observations.js",
  "content": "#!/usr/bin/env node\n/**\n * Backfill [Raw] observations by re-summarizing them through the LLM CLI proxy.\n * Run from the coding project root: node scripts/backfill-raw-observations.js\n */\nimport Database from 'better-sqlite3';\nimport path from 'path';\nimport { fileURLToPath } from 'url';\n\nconst __dirname = path.dirname(fileURLToPath(import.<COMPANY_NAME_REDACTED>.url));\nconst DB_PATH = path.resolve(__dirname, '../.observations/observations.db');\nconst PROXY_PORT = process.env.LLM_CLI_PROXY_PORT || '12435';\nconst PROXY_URL = `http://localhost:${PROXY_PORT}/api/complete`;\nconst BATCH_DELAY_MS = 2000;\n\nconst db = new Database(DB_PATH);\n\nconst rawObs = db.prepare(`\n  SELECT id, summary, messages, metadata, created_at\n  FROM observations\n  WHERE summary LIKE '[Raw] % messages%'\n  ORDER BY created_at ASC\n`).all();\n\nprocess.stderr.write(`Found ${rawObs.length} [Raw] observations to backfill\\n`);\n\nlet success = 0, failed = 0, skipped = 0;\n\nfor (let i = 0; i < rawObs.length; i++) {\n  const obs = rawObs[i];\n\n  let messages;\n  try { messages = JSON.parse(obs.messages); }\n  catch { skipped++; continue; }\n\n  if (!messages || messages.length < 2) { skipped++; continue; }\n\n  let metadata = {};\n  try { metadata = JSON.parse(obs.metadata || '{}'); } catch { /* ignore */ }\n  const projectName = metadata.project || 'coding';\n\n  const exchangeBlock = messages\n    .map(m => `<${m.role}>\\n${m.content}\\n</${m.role}>`)\n    .join('\\n');\n\n  const modifiedFiles = metadata.modifiedFiles || [];\n  let artifactHint = '';\n  if (modifiedFiles.length > 0) {\n    artifactHint = `\\n\\nGROUND TRUTH — Files modified/created:\\n` +\n      modifiedFiles.map(f => `  - edited ${f}`).join('\\n');\n  }\n\n  const requestBody = {\n    messages: [\n      {\n        role: 'system',\n        content: `You produce structured observation summaries from coding exchanges.\\n` +\n          `The developer is working in the \"${projectName}\" project.\\n\\n` +\n          'Respond using ONLY this template:\\n\\n' +\n          'Intent: [what the developer asked]\\n' +\n          'Approach: [solution strategy — 1-4 sentences]\\n' +\n          'Artifacts: [files modified/created with verb, or \"none\"]\\n' +\n          'Result: [concrete outcome — 1-4 sentences]\\n\\n' +\n          'If no real work, respond: \"No actionable content.\"' +\n          (artifactHint || ''),\n      },\n      {\n        role: 'user',\n        content: `<project>${projectName}</project>\\n<exchange>\\n${exchangeBlock}\\n</exchange>\\n\\nProduce the observation summary.`,\n      },\n    ],\n  };\n\n  try {\n    const response = await fetch(PROXY_URL, {\n      method: 'POST',\n      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },\n      body: JSON.stringify(requestBody),\n      signal: AbortSignal.timeout(45000),\n    });\n\n    if (!response.ok) {\n      const errBody = await response.text();\n      process.stderr.write(`  [${i+1}/${rawObs.length}] ERR ${response.status}: ${errBody.slice(0,60)}\\n`);\n      failed++;\n      continue;\n    }\n\n    const result = await response.json();\n    const summary = result.content;\n\n    if (!summary || summary.length < 10) { skipped++; continue; }\n\n    const <USER_ID_REDACTED> = summary.toLowerCase().includes('no actionable content') ? WHERE id = ?`)\n      .run(summary, JSON.stringify(llmMeta), <USER_ID_REDACTED>, obs.id);\n\n    process.stderr.write(`  [${i+1}/${rawObs.length}] ${<USER_ID_REDACTED> === 'low' ? 'LOW' : 'OK'}: ${obs.created_at.slice(0,19)} — ${summary.slice(0,50)}\\n`);\n    success++;\n  } catch (err) {\n    process.stderr.write(`  [${i+1}/${rawObs.length}] FAIL: ${err.message}\\n`);\n    failed++;\n  }\n\n  if (i < rawObs.length - 1) {\n    await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, BATCH_DELAY_MS));\n  }\n}\n\nprocess.stderr.write(`\\nDone: ${success} updated, ${failed} failed, ${skipped} skipped\\n`);\ndb.close();\n"
}

### Write - 2026-04-12 06:14:20 UTC [08:14:20 CEST]

**User Request:** yes

**Tool:** Write
**Input:** ```json
{
  "file_path": "/tmp/backfill-observations.js",
  "content": "/**\n * Backfill [Raw] observations by re-summarizing them through the LLM proxy.\n * Reads the stored messages from the DB, calls the proxy, updates the summary.\n */\nimport Database from 'better-sqlite3';\nimport path from 'path';\n\nconst DB_PATH = path.resolve('/Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/coding/.observations/observations.db');\nconst PROXY_PORT = process.env.LLM_CLI_PROXY_PORT || '12435';\nconst PROXY_URL = `http://localhost:${PROXY_PORT}/api/complete`;\nconst BATCH_DELAY_MS = 2000; // Rate limit between calls\n\nconst db = new Database(DB_PATH);\n\n// Get all [Raw] observations that have stored messages\nconst rawObs = db.prepare(`\n  SELECT id, summary, messages, metadata, created_at\n  FROM observations\n  WHERE summary LIKE '[Raw] % messages%'\n  ORDER BY created_at ASC\n`).all();\n\nprocess.stderr.write(`Found ${rawObs.length} [Raw] observations to backfill\\n`);\n\nlet success = 0;\nlet failed = 0;\nlet skipped = 0;\n\nfor (let i = 0; i < rawObs.length; i++) {\n  const obs = rawObs[i];\n\n  // Parse stored messages\n  let messages;\n  try {\n    messages = JSON.parse(obs.messages);\n  } catch (_e) {\n    process.stderr.write(`  [${i+1}/${rawObs.length}] SKIP: cannot parse messages for ${obs.id}\\n`);\n    skipped++;\n    continue;\n  }\n\n  if (!messages || messages.length < 2) {\n    skipped++;\n    continue;\n  }\n\n  // Parse metadata for project name\n  let metadata = {};\n  try {\n    metadata = JSON.parse(obs.metadata || '{}');\n  } catch (_e) {\n    // ignore\n  }\n  const projectName = metadata.project || 'coding';\n\n  // Build exchange block\n  const exchangeBlock = messages\n    .map(m => `<${m.role}>\\n${m.content}\\n</${m.role}>`)\n    .join('\\n');\n\n  // Build ground-truth file list from metadata\n  const modifiedFiles = metadata.modifiedFiles || [];\n  const readFiles = metadata.readFiles || [];\n  let artifactHint = '';\n  if (modifiedFiles.length > 0) {\n    artifactHint = `\\n\\nGROUND TRUTH — Files modified/created by tool calls (use these for the Artifacts line):\\n` +\n      modifiedFiles.map(f => `  - edited ${f}`).join('\\n');\n  }\n\n  const requestBody = {\n    messages: [\n      {\n        role: 'system',\n        content: `You produce structured observation summaries from coding exchanges.\\n` +\n          `CRITICAL CONTEXT: The developer is working in the \"${projectName}\" project.\\n\\n` +\n          'Respond using ONLY this template — nothing else:\\n\\n' +\n          'Intent: [what the developer actually asked or requested]\\n' +\n          'Approach: [architectural decisions, solution strategy — 1-4 sentences]\\n' +\n          'Artifacts: [list each file modified/created/deleted with verb. Write \"none\" if no files were touched]\\n' +\n          'Result: [the concrete solution or outcome — 1-4 sentences]\\n\\n' +\n          'Constraints:\\n' +\n          '- Your ENTIRE response must be these 4 labeled lines.\\n' +\n          '- Never reproduce code, commands, or file contents.\\n' +\n          '- If the exchange has no real work (greetings, \"yes\", \"proceed\"), respond with only: \"No actionable content.\"' +\n          (artifactHint || ''),\n      },\n      {\n        role: 'user',\n        content: `<project>${projectName}</project>\\n<exchange>\\n${exchangeBlock}\\n</exchange>\\n\\nProduce the observation summary.`,\n      },\n    ],\n  };\n\n  try {\n    const response = await fetch(PROXY_URL, {\n      method: 'POST',\n      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },\n      body: JSON.stringify(requestBody),\n      signal: AbortSignal.timeout(45000),\n    });\n\n    if (!response.ok) {\n      const errBody = await response.text();\n      process.stderr.write(`  [${i+1}/${rawObs.length}] ERROR ${response.status}: ${errBody.slice(0,80)}\\n`);\n      failed++;\n      continue;\n    }\n\n    const result = await response.json();\n    const summary = result.content;\n\n    if (!summary || summary.length < 10) {\n      process.stderr.write(`  [${i+1}/${rawObs.length}] SKIP: empty summary\\n`);\n      skipped++;\n      continue;\n    }\n\n    // Skip \"No actionable content\" — these are low-value\n    if (summary.toLowerCase().includes('no actionable content')) {\n      // Update to mark as processed but low-value\n      db.prepare(`UPDATE observations SET summary = ?, <USER_ID_REDACTED> = 'low' WHERE id = ?`)\n        .run(summary, obs.id);\n      process.stderr.write(`  [${i+1}/${rawObs.length}] LOW: ${obs.created_at.slice(0,19)}\\n`);\n      success++;\n      continue;\n    }\n\n    // Update the observation with the new summary and LLM metadata\n    const llmMeta = {\n      ...metadata,\n      llmModel: result.model || null,\n      llmProvider: result.provider || null,\n      llmTokens: result.tokens || null,\n      llmLatencyMs: result.latencyMs || null,\n    };\n\n    db.prepare(`UPDATE observations SET summary = ?, metadata = ?, <USER_ID_REDACTED> = 'normal' WHERE id = ?`)\n      .run(summary, JSON.stringify(llmMeta), obs.id);\n\n    process.stderr.write(`  [${i+1}/${rawObs.length}] OK: ${obs.created_at.slice(0,19)} — ${summary.slice(0,60)}\\n`);\n    success++;\n\n  } catch (err) {\n    process.stderr.write(`  [${i+1}/${rawObs.length}] FAIL: ${err.message}\\n`);\n    failed++;\n  }\n\n  // Rate limit\n  if (i < rawObs.length - 1) {\n    await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, BATCH_DELAY_MS));\n  }\n}\n\nprocess.stderr.write(`\\nBackfill complete: ${success} updated, ${failed} failed, ${skipped} skipped\\n`);\ndb.close();\n"
}
```

**Input:** ```json
{
  "file_path": "/tmp/backfill-observations.js",
  "content": "/**\n * Backfill [Raw] observations by re-summarizing them through the LLM proxy.\n * Reads the stored messages from the DB, calls the proxy, updates the summary.\n */\nimport Database from 'better-sqlite3';\nimport path from 'path';\n\nconst DB_PATH = path.resolve('/Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/coding/.observations/observations.db');\nconst PROXY_PORT = process.env.LLM_CLI_PROXY_PORT || '12435';\nconst PROXY_URL = `http://localhost:${PROXY_PORT}/api/complete`;\nconst BATCH_DELAY_MS = 2000; // Rate limit between calls\n\nconst db = new Database(DB_PATH);\n\n// Get all [Raw] observations that have stored messages\nconst rawObs = db.prepare(`\n  SELECT id, summary, messages, metadata, created_at\n  FROM observations\n  WHERE summary LIKE '[Raw] % messages%'\n  ORDER BY created_at ASC\n`).all();\n\nprocess.stderr.write(`Found ${rawObs.length} [Raw] observations to backfill\\n`);\n\nlet success = 0;\nlet failed = 0;\nlet skipped = 0;\n\nfor (let i = 0; i < rawObs.length; i++) {\n  const obs = rawObs[i];\n\n  // Parse stored messages\n  let messages;\n  try {\n    messages = JSON.parse(obs.messages);\n  } catch (_e) {\n    process.stderr.write(`  [${i+1}/${rawObs.length}] SKIP: cannot parse messages for ${obs.id}\\n`);\n    skipped++;\n    continue;\n  }\n\n  if (!messages || messages.length < 2) {\n    skipped++;\n    continue;\n  }\n\n  // Parse metadata for project name\n  let metadata = {};\n  try {\n    metadata = JSON.parse(obs.metadata || '{}');\n  } catch (_e) {\n    // ignore\n  }\n  const projectName = metadata.project || 'coding';\n\n  // Build exchange block\n  const exchangeBlock = messages\n    .map(m => `<${m.role}>\\n${m.content}\\n</${m.role}>`)\n    .join('\\n');\n\n  // Build ground-truth file list from metadata\n  const modifiedFiles = metadata.modifiedFiles || [];\n  const readFiles = metadata.readFiles || [];\n  let artifactHint = '';\n  if (modifiedFiles.length > 0) {\n    artifactHint = `\\n\\nGROUND TRUTH — Files modified/created by tool calls (use these for the Artifacts line):\\n` +\n      modifiedFiles.map(f => `  - edited ${f}`).join('\\n');\n  }\n\n  const requestBody = {\n    messages: [\n      {\n        role: 'system',\n        content: `You produce structured observation summaries from coding exchanges.\\n` +\n          `CRITICAL CONTEXT: The developer is working in the \"${projectName}\" project.\\n\\n` +\n          'Respond using ONLY this template — nothing else:\\n\\n' +\n          'Intent: [what the developer actually asked or requested]\\n' +\n          'Approach: [architectural decisions, solution strategy — 1-4 sentences]\\n' +\n          'Artifacts: [list each file modified/created/deleted with verb. Write \"none\" if no files were touched]\\n' +\n          'Result: [the concrete solution or outcome — 1-4 sentences]\\n\\n' +\n          'Constraints:\\n' +\n          '- Your ENTIRE response must be these 4 labeled lines.\\n' +\n          '- Never reproduce code, commands, or file contents.\\n' +\n          '- If the exchange has no real work (greetings, \"yes\", \"proceed\"), respond with only: \"No actionable content.\"' +\n          (artifactHint || ''),\n      },\n      {\n        role: 'user',\n        content: `<project>${projectName}</project>\\n<exchange>\\n${exchangeBlock}\\n</exchange>\\n\\nProduce the observation summary.`,\n      },\n    ],\n  };\n\n  try {\n    const response = await fetch(PROXY_URL, {\n      method: 'POST',\n      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },\n      body: JSON.stringify(requestBody),\n      signal: AbortSignal.timeout(45000),\n    });\n\n    if (!response.ok) {\n      const errBody = await response.text();\n      process.stderr.write(`  [${i+1}/${rawObs.length}] ERROR ${response.status}: ${errBody.slice(0,80)}\\n`);\n      failed++;\n      continue;\n    }\n\n    const result = await response.json();\n    const summary = result.content;\n\n    if (!summary || summary.length < 10) {\n      process.stderr.write(`  [${i+1}/${rawObs.length}] SKIP: empty summary\\n`);\n      skipped++;\n      continue;\n    }\n\n    // Skip \"No actionable content\" — these are low-value\n    if (summary.toLowerCase().includes('no actionable content')) {\n      // Update to mark as processed but low-value\n      db.prepare(`UPDATE observations SET summary = ?, <USER_ID_REDACTED> = 'low' WHERE id = ?`)\n        .run(summary, obs.id);\n      process.stderr.write(`  [${i+1}/${rawObs.length}] LOW: ${obs.created_at.slice(0,19)}\\n`);\n      success++;\n      continue;\n    }\n\n    // Update the observation with the new summary and LLM metadata\n    const llmMeta = {\n      ...metadata,\n      llmModel: result.model || null,\n      llmProvider: result.provider || null,\n      llmTokens: result.tokens || null,\n      llmLatencyMs: result.latencyMs || null,\n    };\n\n    db.prepare(`UPDATE observations SET summary = ?, metadata = ?, <USER_ID_REDACTED> = 'normal' WHERE id = ?`)\n      .run(summary, JSON.stringify(llmMeta), obs.id);\n\n    process.stderr.write(`  [${i+1}/${rawObs.length}] OK: ${obs.created_at.slice(0,19)} — ${summary.slice(0,60)}\\n`);\n    success++;\n\n  } catch (err) {\n    process.stderr.write(`  [${i+1}/${rawObs.length}] FAIL: ${err.message}\\n`);\n    failed++;\n  }\n\n  // Rate limit\n  if (i < rawObs.length - 1) {\n    await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, BATCH_DELAY_MS));\n  }\n}\n\nprocess.stderr.write(`\\nBackfill complete: ${success} updated, ${failed} failed, ${skipped} skipped\\n`);\ndb.close();\n"
}
```

**Result:** ✅ Success
**Output:** ```
File created successfully at: /tmp/backfill-observations.js
```

{\n      method: 'POST',\n      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },\n      body: JSON.stringify(requestBody),\n      signal: AbortSignal.timeout(45000),\n    });\n\n    if (!response.ok) {\n      const errBody = await response.text();\n      process.stderr.write(`  [${i+1}/${rawObs.length}] ERROR ${response.status}: ${errBody.slice(0,80)}\\n`);\n      failed++;\n      continue;\n    }\n\n    const result = await response.json();\n    const summary = result.content;\n\n    if (!summary || summary.length < 10) {\n      process.stderr.write(`  [${i+1}/${rawObs.length}] SKIP: empty summary\\n`);\n      skipped++;\n      continue;\n    }\n\n    // Skip \"No actionable content\" — these are low-value\n    if (summary.toLowerCase().includes('no actionable content')) {\n      // Update to mark as processed but low-value\n      db.prepare(`UPDATE observations SET summary = ?, <USER_ID_REDACTED> = 'low' WHERE id = ?`)\n        .run(summary, obs.id);\n      process.stderr.write(`  [${i+1}/${rawObs.length}] LOW: ${obs.created_at.slice(0,19)}\\n`);\n      success++;\n      continue;\n    }\n\n    // Update the observation with the new summary and LLM metadata\n    const llmMeta = {\n      ...metadata,\n      llmModel: result.model || null,\n      llmProvider: result.provider || null,\n      llmTokens: result.tokens || null,\n      llmLatencyMs: result.latencyMs || null,\n    };\n\n    db.prepare(`UPDATE observations SET summary = ?, metadata = ?, <USER_ID_REDACTED> = 'normal' WHERE id = ?`)\n      .run(summary, JSON.stringify(llmMeta), obs.id);\n\n    process.stderr.write(`  [${i+1}/${rawObs.length}] OK: ${obs.created_at.slice(0,19)} — ${summary.slice(0,60)}\\n`);\n    success++;\n\n  } catch (err) {\n    process.stderr.write(`  [${i+1}/${rawObs.length}] FAIL: ${err.message}\\n`);\n    failed++;\n  }\n\n  // Rate limit\n  if (i < rawObs.length - 1) {\n    await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, BATCH_DELAY_MS));\n  }\n}\n\nprocess.stderr.write(`\\nBackfill complete: ${success} updated, ${failed} failed, ${skipped} skipped\\n`);\ndb.close();\n"
}
```

**Result:** ✅ Success
**Output:** ```
File created successfully at: /tmp/backfill-observations.js
```

### Write - 2026-04-12 06:14:20 UTC [08:14:20 CEST]

**User Request:** yes

**Tool:** Write
**Input:** ```json
{
  "file_path": "<AWS_SECRET_REDACTED>ckfill-raw-observations.js",
  "content": "#!/usr/bin/env node\n/**\n * Backfill [Raw] observations by re-summarizing them through the LLM CLI proxy.\n * Run from the coding project root: node scripts/backfill-raw-observations.js\n */\nimport Database from 'better-sqlite3';\nimport path from 'path';\nimport { fileURLToPath } from 'url';\n\nconst __dirname = path.dirname(fileURLToPath(import.<COMPANY_NAME_REDACTED>.url));\nconst DB_PATH = path.resolve(__dirname, '../.observations/observations.db');\nconst PROXY_PORT = process.env.LLM_CLI_PROXY_PORT || '12435';\nconst PROXY_URL = `http://localhost:${PROXY_PORT}/api/complete`;\nconst BATCH_DELAY_MS = 2000;\n\nconst db = new Database(DB_PATH);\n\nconst rawObs = db.prepare(`\n  SELECT id, summary, messages, metadata, created_at\n  FROM observations\n  WHERE summary LIKE '[Raw] % messages%'\n  ORDER BY created_at ASC\n`).all();\n\nprocess.stderr.write(`Found ${rawObs.length} [Raw] observations to backfill\\n`);\n\nlet success = 0, failed = 0, skipped = 0;\n\nfor (let i = 0; i < rawObs.length; i++) {\n  const obs = rawObs[i];\n\n  let messages;\n  try { messages = JSON.parse(obs.messages); }\n  catch { skipped++; continue; }\n\n  if (!messages || messages.length < 2) { skipped++; continue; }\n\n  let metadata = {};\n  try { metadata = JSON.parse(obs.metadata || '{}'); } catch { /* ignore */ }\n  const projectName = metadata.project || 'coding';\n\n  const exchangeBlock = messages\n    .map(m => `<${m.role}>\\n${m.content}\\n</${m.role}>`)\n    .join('\\n');\n\n  const modifiedFiles = metadata.modifiedFiles || [];\n  let artifactHint = '';\n  if (modifiedFiles.length > 0) {\n    artifactHint = `\\n\\nGROUND TRUTH — Files modified/created:\\n` +\n      modifiedFiles.map(f => `  - edited ${f}`).join('\\n');\n  }\n\n  const requestBody = {\n    messages: [\n      {\n        role: 'system',\n        content: `You produce structured observation summaries from coding exchanges.\\n` +\n          `The developer is working in the \"${projectName}\" project.\\n\\n` +\n          'Respond using ONLY this template:\\n\\n' +\n          'Intent: [what the developer asked]\\n' +\n          'Approach: [solution strategy — 1-4 sentences]\\n' +\n          'Artifacts: [files modified/created with verb, or \"none\"]\\n' +\n          'Result: [concrete outcome — 1-4 sentences]\\n\\n' +\n          'If no real work, respond: \"No actionable content.\"' +\n          (artifactHint || ''),\n      },\n      {\n        role: 'user',\n        content: `<project>${projectName}</project>\\n<exchange>\\n${exchangeBlock}\\n</exchange>\\n\\nProduce the observation summary.`,\n      },\n    ],\n  };\n\n  try {\n    const response = await fetch(PROXY_URL, {\n      method: 'POST',\n      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },\n      body: JSON.stringify(requestBody),\n      signal: AbortSignal.timeout(45000),\n    });\n\n    if (!response.ok) {\n      const errBody = await response.text();\n      process.stderr.write(`  [${i+1}/${rawObs.length}] ERR ${response.status}: ${errBody.slice(0,60)}\\n`);\n      failed++;\n      continue;\n    }\n\n    const result = await response.json();\n    const summary = result.content;\n\n    if (!summary || summary.length < 10) { skipped++; continue; }\n\n    const <USER_ID_REDACTED> = summary.toLowerCase().includes('no actionable content') ? 'low' : 'normal';\n    const llmMeta = {\n      ...metadata,\n      llmModel: result.model || null,\n      llmProvider: result.provider || null,\n      llmTokens: result.tokens || null,\n      llmLatencyMs: result.latencyMs || null,\n    };\n\n    db.prepare(`UPDATE observations SET summary = ?, metadata = ?, <USER_ID_REDACTED> = ? WHERE id = ?`)\n      .run(summary, JSON.stringify(llmMeta), <USER_ID_REDACTED>, obs.id);\n\n    process.stderr.write(`  [${i+1}/${rawObs.length}] ${<USER_ID_REDACTED> === 'low' ? 'LOW' : 'OK'}: ${obs.created_at.slice(0,19)} — ${summary.slice(0,50)}\\n`);\n    success++;\n  } catch (err) {\n    process.stderr.write(`  [${i+1}/${rawObs.length}] FAIL: ${err.message}\\n`);\n    failed++;\n  }\n\n  if (i < rawObs.length - 1) {\n    await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, BATCH_DELAY_MS));\n  }\n}\n\nprocess.stderr.write(`\\nDone: ${success} updated, ${failed} failed, ${skipped} skipped\\n`);\ndb.close();\n"
}
```
